# TEERTHANKER MAHAVEER UNIVERSITY (TMU) — COMPLETE KNOWLEDGE BASE

## University Overview
Teerthanker Mahaveer University (TMU) is a premier private university located in Moradabad, Uttar Pradesh, India. Established in 2008, it is spread across a 140-acre lush green campus on Delhi Road (NH-24). TMU is NAAC 'A' Grade accredited and UGC approved. It offers 200+ programmes across 15+ colleges.

Key Highlights:
- NAAC 'A' Grade accredited
- 140-acre green campus in Moradabad, UP
- 15+ colleges including Engineering, Medical, Dental, Pharmacy, Law, Management, Nursing, Paramedical, Agriculture, Fine Arts, Education, and more
- 100% placement assistance with top recruiters like TCS, Wipro, Infosys, HCL, Deloitte, HDFC
- Highest package: 60 LPA, Average package: 5-7 LPA
- State-of-the-art labs, smart classrooms, and research facilities
- Well-equipped hostels (separate for boys and girls), mess, gym, sports complex
- 24x7 security with CCTV cameras and dedicated wardens
- Strong alumni network of 50,000+ graduates
- Founded by Suresh Jain, a visionary educationist

## TMU Contact Information
- Admission Helpline: 9568918000 / 9568917000
- Website: https://www.tmu.ac.in
- Brochure: https://rebrand.ly/TMU-brochure
- Address: Delhi Road (NH-24), Moradabad - 244001, Uttar Pradesh, India

## Campus Facilities
- Central Library with 1 lakh+ books and digital resources
- Wi-Fi enabled campus
- Sports: Cricket, Football, Basketball, Badminton, Swimming, Gym, Table Tennis
- Cafeterias and food courts
- ATM, medical clinic on campus
- Transportation facility available
- Auditorium and seminar halls

## Hostel Information
- Separate hostels for boys and girls
- Pure vegetarian mess with weekly changing menu
- 24x7 security with CCTV
- Wi-Fi in hostels
- Warden and caretaker available round the clock
- Gate pass system for safety
- Hostel fees: approximately 60,000-80,000 per year (varies)

## Scholarships
- 50% tuition fee waiver for Jain Minority students
- Merit Scholarship for 12th >90% marks
- Sports Quota scholarship available
- UP Government scholarship applicable
- SC/ST/OBC scholarships as per government norms

## Placement Record
- 100% placement assistance
- 600+ companies visit campus annually
- Highest package: 60 LPA
- Average package: 5-7 LPA
- Top recruiters: TCS, Wipro, Infosys, HCL, Deloitte, HDFC, ICICI, Byju's, Amazon, Flipkart
- Pre-placement training, mock interviews, and soft skill workshops

## Anti-Ragging Policy
- TMU is a 100% Ragging-Free campus
- Anti-Ragging Committee is active
- Strict laws and immediate action on complaints
- Senior students follow a 'Didi/Bhaiya' culture — very supportive

## Popular Programmes at TMU
- B.Tech (CSE, ME, CE, EE, ECE) — 4 years
- BCA — 3 years
- MCA — 2 years
- MBA — 2 years
- BBA — 3 years
- MBBS — 5.5 years
- BDS — 5 years
- B.Pharm — 4 years
- B.Sc Nursing — 4 years
- LLB — 3/5 years
- B.Ed — 2 years
- B.Sc Agriculture — 4 years
- And 200+ more programmes



# COMMON STUDENT FAQS (HINGLISH)



# COMMON ADMISSION FAQS (HINGLISH)

Q: Placement kaisa hai? Job lag jayegi pakka?
A: Dekhiye, TMU ka placement record shandaar hai. Highest package 60 LPA raha hai. Average package 5-7 LPA rehta hai. 100% placement assistance milti hai. Agar student mehnat kare, toh job pakka lagti hai. Top recruiters mein TCS, Wipro, Infosys included hain.

Q: Hostel ka khana kaisa hai?
A: Hostel mein sirf Pure Veg khana milta hai, jo ghar jaisa hygienic hota hai. Menu weekly change hota hai - Dal makhani, Paneer, Roti, Rice sab milta hai. Mess safai ka poora dhyan rakhti hai.

Q: Girls ke liye safety kaisi hai?
A: Safety hamari top priority hai. Campus poori tarah secure hai - 24x7 guards aur CCTV cameras lage hain. Girls hostel campus ke andar hi hai aur warden ki strict monitoring rehti hai. Entry-exit timings fix hain. Parents can rest assured.

Q: Kya direct admission ho jayega bina exam ke?
A: Kuch courses mein merit-based (12th marks) direct admission hota hai. Lekin technical courses (jaise B.Tech) ke liye JEE ya TMU ka entrance test dena pad sakta hai. Aap apne marks bataiye, main check kar lungi.

Q: Koi scholarship ya discount milega?
A: Haan ji, bilkul!
1. Jain Minority students ke liye 50% tuition fee waiver hai.
2. Merit Scholarship: 12th mein >90% marks par scholarship milti hai.
3. Sports quota bhi available hai.
Aapka koi category lagta hai kya?

Q: Ragging hoti hai kya campus mein?
A: Bilkul nahi! TMU ek 100% Ragging-Free campus hai. Strict laws hain aur Anti-Ragging committee active rehti hai. Senior students bahut supportive hain 'Didi/Bhaiya' wala culture hai.

Q: Mobile phone allowed hai hostel mein?
A: Haan ji, mobile phones allowed hain. Bas class timings mein silent rakhna hota hai. Pure campus mein Wi-Fi connectivity bhi available hai.

Q: Weekend pe bahar ja sakte hain?
A: Sunday ko outing allowed hoti hai lekin specific timings ke sath. First year students ke liye gate pass system hota hai jisme parents ki permission lag sakti hai. Safety ke liye yeh zaroori hai.

Q: Uniform pehenni padegi kya?
A: Haan, professional environment maintain karne ke liye uniform compulsory hai. Isse discipline aur equality bani rehti hai.

Q: Moradabad kaise pahunch sakte hain campus?
A: TMU campus Delhi Road (NH-24) par hai. Moradabad Railway station se bas 10-15 km door hai. Auto aur cabs easily mil jate hain. Delhi se drive karke 3-3.5 ghante lagte hain.

Q: Syllabus tough toh nahi hai? Hindi medium se hoon.
A: Chinta mat kijiye! Teachers bahut supportive hain aur Hindi-English mix mein samjhate hain. Initially bridge classes bhi hoti hain taaki Hindi medium students ko dikkat na aaye.



# ABOUT  MD PAEDIATRICS.DOCX

📘 Course Overview – MD Paediatrics

Q1: What is MD Paediatrics?
 Q2: MD Paediatrics kya hai?
 Q3: What does the course cover?
 Q4: Course me kya-kya sikhaya jata hai?
 Q5: Is it a clinical programme?
 Q6: Kya yeh clinical programme hai?

A:
 MD Paediatrics is a 3-year clinical postgraduate programme focused on the healthcare of infants, children, and adolescents. It trains students in diagnosis, treatment, and child health management from birth to 18 years.
 For more information, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/programme/md-paediatrics
 For admission help, call: 9568518000

 To apply for MD Paediatrics, candidates must have an MBBS degree and permanent registration with the Medical Council of India or a State Medical Council.

 BPharm (Bachelor of Pharmacy) is a 4-year undergraduate programme covering pharmaceutical sciences, drug formulation, pharmacology, and chemistry. It prepares students for careers in hospitals, pharmaceutical companies, research, and clinical roles.

# ABOUT MBBS BACHELOR OF MEDICINE BACHELOR OF SURGERY.DOCX

 MBBS at TMU is a UG programme of 4.5 years + 1‑year mandatory internship, focusing on quality medical education and research-based learning.
 More details & online application: https://admissions.tmu.ac.in/ or call 9568518000.



✅ Eligibility for MBBS

✅ Eligibility for MBBS

Q1: What is the eligibility for MBBS?
 Q2: MBBS में एडमिशन के लिए क्या पात्रता है?
 Q3: Do I need Physics, Chemistry, and Biology?
 Q4: क्या Physics, Chemistry, और Biology जरूरी है?
 Q5: What percentage is required for admission?
 Q6: एडमिशन के लिए न्यूनतम कितने प्रतिशत अंक चाहिए?

Ans:
Eligibility Criteria
 Candidates must have passed 10+2 with Physics, Chemistry, and Biology (PCB), achieving a minimum of 50% marks in aggregate and a pass mark in English.

Criteria of Merit
 Admission to the MBBS programme is strictly based on NEET‑UG merit.

Have questions about the eligibility or admission process? Contact our Admissions Team at 9568518000 or visit the portal: https://admissions.tmu.ac.in/

# ABOUT MD DERMATOLOGY.DOCX

Course Overview – MD Dermatology

Q1: What is MD in Dermatology?

 Q5: Is it a clinical course?
 Q6: Kya yeh clinical programme hai?

 MD Dermatology, Venereology & Leprosy is a 3-year clinical PG programme focused on the diagnosis and treatment of skin, hair, nail, and venereal diseases. It also includes minor surgical procedures and cosmetic dermatology.

# B.COM HONOURS  HONOURS WITH RESEARCH.DOCX

B.Com (Honours / Honours with Research)

Tell me about B.Com (Honours / Honours with Research)

B.Com (Honours) programme is a four-year undergraduate programme designed to provide students with in-depth knowledge of commerce, finance, and business practices

. With a curriculum that blends theoretical understanding with practical application, B.Com (Hons) equips students with the essential skills needed for a successful career in the corporate world or higher studies like CA, CMA, MBA, and more.The programme offers multiple industry-relevant specialisations, allowing students to focus on areas that align with their career goals

. TMU’s experienced faculty, modern infrastructure, and practical learning approach ensure that students graduate industry-ready.

, neural networks, and AI-driven decision-making tools.E-Commerce and Digital MarketingFocuses on the principles of online business models, e-commerce platforms, and effective digital marketing strategies.Helps students understand consumer behavior, online advertising techniques, and digital branding to drive business growth.Big Data and AnalyticsProvides in-depth knowledge of data analysis

Frequently Asked Questions about BElEd (Bachelor of Elementary Education)

Q: Full Form Of B.El.Ed

A: It’s important to understand the nomenclature: B.El.Ed stands for Bachelor of Elementary Education, a programme that merges educational theory and practical training for future elementary school teachers.

Q: Highlights of the programme

Q: Highlights of the programme

A: TMU's B.El.Ed programme provides top-tier training for teaching, educational consultancy, and curriculum design. It adopts an interdisciplinary approach, combining theoretical knowledge with practical applications. TMU equips graduates for advanced studies and specialisation in areas like special education and early childhood education.

Q: Why Choose B.El.Ed (Integrated) programme?

A: Choosing a Bachelor of Elementary Education (B.El.Ed) integrated programme can be beneficial for several reasons:Holistic Education ApproachThe B.El.Ed programme is designed to provide a comprehensive understanding of elementary education, combining theoretical knowledge with practical training

. This holistic approach prepares students to be effective educators for young children.Integrated CurriculumUnlike traditional education degrees, the B.El.Ed programme integrates education theory, pedagogy, and practical experience from the start

. This integration helps students develop a deep understanding of child development, learning processes, and teaching methodologies.Professional QualificationCompleting a B.El.Ed programme provides a recognised professional qualification that enables graduates to teach at the elementary level

. This degree is often a requirement for teaching positions in primary schools.Career OpportunitiesGraduates of the B.El.Ed programme can pursue various career paths in the education sector, including teaching in schools, educational consultancy, curriculum design, educational research, and administration

. The programme also provides a solid foundation for further studies in education or related fields.Focus on Child DevelopmentThe B.El.Ed curriculum places a strong emphasis on understanding the cognitive, emotional, and social development of children

. This focus equips future educators with the skills to create nurturing and effective learning environments.Hands-on ExperienceThe programme includes extensive practical training through internships, teaching practice, and classroom observations. This hands-on experience is invaluable in preparing students for real-world teaching challenges.

Q: Skills Required for B.El.Ed Students

A: Students pursuing a Bachelor of Elementary Education (B.El.Ed) programme need to develop a diverse set of skills to succeed in their studies and future teaching careers.Some key skills required include:Communication SkillsCommunication skills refer to the ability to effectively convey information, ideas, and instructions to others

. In an educational setting, this includes both verbal and written communication. Teachers use these skills to explain concepts clearly, engage students, and foster a positive learning environment

. Strong communication also involves active listening, ensuring that teachers understand and address students' questions and concerns.Teaching AptitudeTeaching aptitude is the natural ability or talent to teach effectively

. This encompasses a range of skills including the ability to explain complex concepts in a simple manner, adapt teaching methods to suit different learning styles, and inspire and motivate students. It involves a passion for education and a genuine interest in helping students learn and grow.Interpersonal SkillsInterpersonal skills involve the ability to interact effectively with others

. For educators, this means building positive relationships with students, colleagues, and parents

. Good interpersonal skills help in understanding and addressing the needs and concerns of students, collaborating with other staff members, and creating a supportive and inclusive classroom environment.Classroom ManagementClassroom management refers to the techniques and strategies used to maintain a productive and orderly learning environment

. This includes setting clear rules and expectations, managing student behaviour, organising classroom activities, and ensuring that lessons are conducted smoothly. Effective classroom management helps minimise disruptions and maximise student engagement and learning.Organizational SkillsOrganisational skills are essential for planning and executing tasks efficiently

. In an educational context, this includes preparing lesson plans, managing classroom materials, and keeping track of student progress and administrative tasks

. Strong organisational skills help teachers maintain a structured and effective learning environment and ensure that all educational objectives are met.Technology ProficiencyTechnology proficiency refers to the ability to effectively use technology tools and resources in teaching

. This includes using educational software, digital resources, and online platforms to enhance learning and engage students. Technology proficiency also involves staying updated with technological advancements and integrating them into the classroom to support educational goals and facilitate interactive learning experiences.

Q: TMU’s Faculty of Education College Specialities

A: The Faculty of Education specialises in various fields.Implementation of psychomotor skills.Tailored sessions for both slow and fast learners.Integration of compulsory value-added programmes into the curriculum.Guidance and practice sessions for government jobs and examinations such as TGT, PGT, TET, CTET, Super TET

, PGT, TET, CTET, Super TET, etc.Mandatory inclusion of MOOCs (Massive Open Online Courses) in the curriculum.Publication of 16 books and 19 edited books by various faculty members.Regular educational talks addressing emerging issues.

Frequently Asked Questions about BTech (AICTE Approved) in Computer Science & Engineering

Q: What is the Full Form of BTech CSE?

A: The full form of BTech CSE is Bachelor of Technology in Computer Science and Engineering. It is a four-year undergraduate degree programme that focuses on the theoretical foundations and practical applications of computing, programming, software development, algorithms, data structures, computer networks, databases, and emerging technologies like AI, machine learning, and cybersecurity.

Q: BTech CSE Eligibility Criteria.

A: To be eligible for admission to the BTech in Computer Science and Engineering (CSE) programme in India, candidates must generally meet the following criteria:Qualification: 10+2 with Physics and Mathematics as compulsory subjects

, along with Chemistry/Computer Science/IT or equivalent.Minimum Marks: 45%–50% aggregate generally (5% relaxation for reserved categories).Entrance Exam: JEE Main/state-level/university-level exam (as applicable).Age: Minimum 17 years; no upper age limit in most cases.Lateral Entry: Diploma holders in engineering may apply for direct admission to 2nd year.

Q: BTech CSE Admission Process

A: The admission process for the BTech in Computer Science and Engineering at Teerthanker Mahaveer University is simple, transparent, and merit-based. Interested candidates can apply through online or offline modes

. Here's a step-by-step breakdown of the process:Eligibility Criteria: 10+2 with Physics, Mathematics, and Chemistry/Computer Science

, with a minimum of 50% aggregate marks.Application Mode: Available both online via the official TMU website and offline at the university campus.Shortlisting: Based on academic merit and entrance exam scores.Counselling & Document Verification: Candidates must participate in the counselling session and verify all required documents.Provisional Admission: Offered upon successful verification and

Offered upon successful verification and selection.Fee Submission: The Final step to confirm the admission.

Q: Admission in BTech CSE at TMU

A: Admission to the B.Tech Computer Science and Engineering (CSE) programme at Teerthanker Mahaveer University (TMU) for the academic year 2025 is currently open

. To begin the admission process, prospective students should first ensure they meet the eligibility criteria, which generally include having passed their 10+2 level examination with physics, mathematics, and either chemistry or computer science as core subjects, securing a minimum of 50% aggregate marks

, securing a minimum of 50% aggregate marks, and passing marks in English from a recognised board.Admission to the BTech CSE programme at TMU is primarily based on the scores obtained in national-level entrance examinations, such as JEE Main or the Common University Entrance Test (CUET)

. Alternatively, candidates may also be shortlisted based on their merit in the qualifying 10+2 examination.

Q: BTech CSE Scope

A: A BTech in Computer Science and Engineering offers vast career potential, both in India and globally

. With rapid digital transformation across industries, CSE graduates are in high demand for roles in IT, software development, data analysis, cybersecurity, and emerging technologies like artificial intelligence and blockchain.Key Areas of Scope:Software Development: Design and develop software applications for various sectors.Data Science & AI: Work in machine learning, data analytics

, data analytics, and AI-based solutions.Cybersecurity: Secure digital infrastructure and prevent cyber threats.Cloud Computing: Develop and manage cloud-based services and platforms.

Q: What is Cloud Computing?

A: Cloud computing is a technology that enables on-demand access to a shared pool of configurable computing resources, such as servers, storage, databases, networking, software, and applications, over the internet. Instead of owning and maintaining physical infrastructure, users can rent computing resources from cloud service providers on a pay-as-you-go basis.

Q: BTech CSE Cloud Computing Eligibility

A: Eligibility criteria for B.Tech in Computer Science and Engineering (CSE) with a specialisation in Cloud Computing in India typically include the following:Qualification: 10+2 (or equivalent) from a recognised board.Subjects Required: Physics, Chemistry

, Chemistry, and Mathematics (PCM) are mandatory.Minimum Marks: 50%–60% aggregate in PCM (relaxation for SC/ST/OBC as per norms).Entrance Exams:National: JEE Main, JEE AdvancedState-level: WBJEE, MHT CET, KCET, etc.

Q: BTech CSE Cloud Computing at TMU

A: Teerthanker Mahaveer University (TMU) in Moradabad, Uttar Pradesh, offers a specialised B.Tech in Computer Science and Engineering (CSE) with a focus on Cloud Technology and Information Security

. This programme is designed to equip students with the skills necessary to excel in the rapidly evolving fields of cloud computing and cybersecurity.TMU is a UGC-recognised, NAAC 'A' grade-accredited, ISO-certified university, with NBA-accredited B.Tech programmes

. The course prepares graduates for roles such as cloud engineer, cybersecurity analyst, and DevOps professional, supported by TMU’s strong industry linkages and dedicated placement assistance.

Q: Frequently Asked Questions (FAQS)

A: Q1: What do you mean by cloud computing?Ans: Cloud computing refers to the delivery of computing services—such as servers, storage, databases, networking, software, analytics, and intelligence—over the internet (commonly called “the cloud”) to offer faster innovation, flexible resources, and economies of scale

. Instead of owning their own computing infrastructure or data centres, organisations can rent access to anything from applications to storage from a cloud service provider like Amazon Web Services (AWS), Microsoft Azure

, Microsoft Azure, or Google Cloud Platform (GCP).Q2: What is the duration of the B.Tech CSE (Cloud Computing) programme at TMU?Ans: The B.Tech in Computer Science and Engineering with a specialisation in Cloud Computing at TMU is a 4-year undergraduate degree programme

, structured across 8 semesters.Q3: What is the eligibility criteria for admission to this course?Ans: Candidates must have passed 10+2 or equivalent in physics, mathematics

, mathematics, and one in chemistry/computer science/information technology with a minimum of 50% marks (45% for SC/ST) to be eligible for admission.Q4: What infrastructure and lab facilities are available for cloud computing students at TMU?Ans: TMU offers all the advanced computing labs required and access to cloud platforms for practical training.

. Generally, a minimum aggregate of 50% marks in PCM is required for general category applicants.

Q: BTech CSE in Data Science at TMU

. The curriculum is designed to equip students with skills in programming, data analysis, machine learning, and big data technologies, preparing them for the evolving demands of the tech industry.To be eligible for this program, candidates must have completed their 10+2 education with Physics, Mathematics, and Chemistry (or Computer Science), securing at least 50% marks and passing in English

. The fee structure includes a tuition fee of ₹61,200 per semester, along with additional charges for examinations, lab usage, and enrollment. TMU also offers scholarships, such as up to 50% tuition fee exemption for Jain students

. Graduates of this program can pursue careers as data scientists, machine learning engineers, data analysts, and other roles in sectors like IT, finance, healthcare, and e-commerce.

 Q3: Can you give a brief overview of the MSc in Optometry programme?
 Q4: MSc in Optometry course mein kis type ka training milta hai?

 MSc in Optometry is a postgraduate programme that trains students in advanced visual health sciences, low vision aids, ocular diagnostics, and clinical procedures. It prepares graduates to serve as skilled optometry professionals in hospitals, clinics, and academia.

# HOSTEL FEES AND ACCOMMODATION.DOCX

Hostel Fees and Accommodation

4 Seater (Common Bath) With Cooler

Q1: What is the hostel fee for a 4-seater room with common bath and cooler (non-Jain)?
 Q2: Jain student ke liye 4-seater common bathroom cooler room ki fee kitni hai?
 Q3: Kya ₹60,000 me mess charge bhi included hai 4-seater common bath room ke liye?
 Q4: 4-seater common bathroom hostel Jain aur non-Jain dono ke liye kitna padta hai?

Q5: Jain students ko kitna discount milta hai 4-seater common bath room pe?
 Q6: Mess charges alag se kitne hain 4-seater common bath with cooler ke liye?
 Q7: Jain ke lodging aur mess breakup kya hai 4-seater common bathroom category me?

Answer:
 For the 4-seater (common bath) with cooler hostel room, the total fee for non-Jain students is ₹60,000 per year, which includes ₹32,000 for lodging and ₹28,000 for mess. For Jain students, the total fee is ₹50,400 per year, including ₹22,400 lodging and ₹28,000 mess. The mess charge is fixed at ₹28,000 per year across all categories and is included in the total hostel fee.

For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/tmu/hostel
 Note: Jain students receive a 30% fee exemption on common bathroom categories and a 15% exemption on attached bathroom categories (lodging only).
 To book your hostel, please call your counsellor. Full payment is required at the time of booking.

4 Seater (Attach Bath) With Cooler

Q1: What is the hostel fee for a 4-seater room with attached bath and cooler (non-Jain)?
 Q2: Jain student ke liye 4-seater attached bathroom cooler room ki fee kitni hai?
 Q3: Kya ₹75,000 me mess bhi included hai 4-seater attached bath category ke liye?
 Q4: Jain aur non-Jain ke liye 4-seater attached bath room ka total cost kya hai?

Q5: Lodging aur mess breakup kya hai Jain students ke liye is category me?
 Q6: Jain students ko kitna discount milta hai 4-seater attached bath hostel me?
 Q7: Kya is category me bhi mess charge fixed hai?

A:
 For the 4-seater (attached bath) with cooler hostel room, the total annual fee for non-Jain students is ₹75,000, which includes ₹47,000 lodging and ₹28,000 mess charges. For Jain students, the total is ₹67,950 per year, with ₹39,950 for lodging and ₹28,000 for mess. Mess charges are fixed and uniform at ₹28,000 per year for all students.

For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/tmu/hostel
 Note: Jain students receive a 30% fee exemption on common bathroom categories and a 15% exemption on attached bathroom categories (lodging only).
 To book your hostel, please call your counsellor. Full payment is required at the time of booking.

3 Seater (Common Bath) With Cooler

Q1: What is the hostel fee for a 3-seater room with common bath and cooler for non-Jain students?
 Q2: Jain student ke liye 3-seater common bathroom cooler room ki total fee kitni hai?
 Q3: Kya ₹80,000 me mess charge included hai is category me?
 Q4: Jain aur non-Jain students ke liye 3-seater common bath category ka breakup kya hai?

Q5: Is category me Jain ko kitna discount milta hai lodging pe?
 Q6: Lodging aur mess ka alag-alag amount kya hai Jain students ke liye?
 Q7: 3-seater common bath with cooler ka mess charge fix hai kya?

A:
 For the 3-seater (common bath) with cooler hostel category, the annual fee for non-Jain students is ₹80,000, which includes ₹52,000 lodging and ₹28,000 mess. For Jain students, the total comes to ₹64,400 annually, consisting of ₹36,400 lodging and ₹28,000 mess. The mess fee of ₹28,000 is fixed for all categories and is already included in the total fee.

For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/tmu/hostel
 Note: Jain students receive a 30% fee exemption on common bathroom categories and a 15% exemption on attached bathroom categories (lodging only).
 To book your hostel, please call your counsellor. Full payment is required at the time of booking.

3 Seater (Attach Bath) With Cooler

Q1: What is the total hostel fee for a 3-seater room with attached bath and cooler (non-Jain)?
 Q2: Jain student ke liye 3-seater attached bathroom cooler room ki poori fee kitni hai?
 Q3: Kya ₹95,000 me mess bhi include hai is hostel category me?
 Q4: 3-seater attached bath room me Jain aur non-Jain ka lodging aur mess breakup kya hai?

Q5: Jain students ko kitna chhoot milta hai is category me?
 Q6: Mess charge fixed hai kya 3-seater attached bath cooler wale room ke liye?
 Q7: Jain students ke liye lodging aur mess kitna alag-alag hai?

A:
 For the 3-seater (attached bath) with cooler room, the annual hostel fee for non-Jain students is ₹95,000, which includes ₹67,000 lodging and ₹28,000 mess. For Jain students, the fee is ₹84,950 per year, comprising ₹56,950 lodging and ₹28,000 mess. The mess charge of ₹28,000 is fixed for all categories and is part of the total amount.

For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/tmu/hostel
 Note: Jain students receive a 30% fee exemption on common bathroom categories and a 15% exemption on attached bathroom categories (lodging only).
 To book your hostel, please call your counsellor. Full payment is required at the time of booking.

2 Seater (Attach Bath) With Cooler

Q1: What is the hostel fee for a 2-seater room with attached bath and cooler (non-Jain)?
 Q2: Jain student ke liye 2-seater attached bathroom cooler room ki fee kitni hai?
 Q3: Kya ₹1,30,000 me mess charges included hain is category ke liye?
 Q4: Jain aur non-Jain students ke liye lodging aur mess ka breakup kya hai?

 For the 2-seater (attached bath) with cooler, the annual hostel fee for non-Jain students is ₹1,30,000, which includes ₹1,02,000 for lodging and ₹28,000 for mess. For Jain students, the total is ₹1,14,700 per year, including ₹86,700 for lodging and ₹28,000 for mess. The mess fee of ₹28,000 is fixed and included in the total amount.

 To book your hostel, please call your counsellor. Full payment is required at the time of booking.


# M PHARM MASTER OF PHARMACY IN PHARMACEUTICS.DOCX

M Pharm (Master of Pharmacy) in Pharmaceutics

Tell me about M Pharm (Master of Pharmacy) in Pharmaceutics

M Pharm (Master of Pharmacy) Pharmaceutics is a two-year postgraduate programme, divided into four semesters. M Pharm Pharmaceutics focuses on the science of drug formulation, development, and manufacturing

. The programme covers a range of subjects or topics such as advanced drug delivery systems, regulatory affairs, and industrial pharmacy. To be eligible for the M Pharm (Master of Pharmacy) Pharmaceutics programme, candidates must hold a Bachelor of Pharmacy (BPharm) degree from a recognised institution or university

, with a minimum aggregate score. M Pharm (Master of Pharmacy) Pharmaceutics programme’s graduates have various career opportunities in the pharmaceutical industry, research and development (R&D), academia, or regulatory bodies, for multiple roles, which makes this an ideal choice for those looking to advance in the pharmaceutical field.

What is the duration of M Pharm (Master of Pharmacy) in Pharmaceutics?

2.0 Years

What is the page URL of M Pharm (Master of Pharmacy) in Pharmaceutics?

https://www.tmu.ac.in/programme/m-pharm-pharmaceutics

What scholarships are available for M Pharm (Master of Pharmacy) in Pharmaceutics?

Scholarship for Jain Students:

Multiple scholarships will not be available.

Chancellor’s Scholarship for Staff Wards

                    District/State/National Level/International Level
Upto 100%
Discount in tuition fee shall be given to the siblings of students

studying/seeking admission in the
                    University with the condition that it will be given to the sibling whose fee is lesser and it
                    shall be
                    applicable on first year tuition fee and not on subsequent years
Upto 10%
Other Scholarship

                        programme. The amount of scholarship shall be such as based upon the level of disability which
                        shall be decided on the basis of certificate of disability (obtained from District Hospital)

being produced. The details of scholarship shall be shared subsequently once decided by the
                        committee constituted for the purpose.
Multiple scholarship will not be available.

Remarks: Scholarships are available in the admission Year
            only. These rules are not applicable on programmes of one year or less than one year duration & Multiple
            scholarships will not be available.

B.Pharm and minimum 50% marks in aggregate.

Frequently Asked Questions about M Pharm (Master of Pharmacy) in Pharmaceutics

Q: Full Form of M.Pharm

Q: Full Form of M.Pharm

A: The full form of M.Pharm. is “Master of Pharmacy in Pharmaceutics”. It is a programme that provides in-depth knowledge of the formulation of drugs, and their development.

Q: Eligibility Criteria for M.Pharm. Pharmaceutics programme

A: To be eligible for the M.Pharm

. Tell me about MD (Doctor of Medicine) in Anatomy

MD (Doctor of Medicine) in Anatomy is a Non Clinical Speciality course. Doctor of Medicine in Anatomy is a three-year postgraduation course. Anatomy is the specialized branch of medicine that deals with the structure of the human body

. , Comparative Anatomy, Physical Anthropology, Radiological Anatomy, Surface Anatomy, Surface marking of Human Body

. Any candidate who has passed the MBBS degree from a recognized University thereto by Medical Council of India or any other State Medical Council is eligible for the course.

MD (Doctor of Medicine) in Pathology is a three-year postgraduate degree related to the field of medicine and diagnostics (the study of disease). . The programme addresses the central three components of disease – the cause, mechanism of development or origin, results of changes. The branch deals with the research of diagnostic, testing and treatment methods with the help of genetic technologies for patient care and prevention of diseases.

MD (Doctor of Medicine) in Pharmacology

Tell me about MD (Doctor of Medicine) in Pharmacology

MD (Doctor of Medicine) in Pharmacology at Teerthanker Mahaveer University is a three-year postgraduate degree that helps students gain fundamental knowledge of biological effects along with therapeutic and chemical uses of drugs. . # MD DOCTOR OF MEDICINE IN PHYSIOLOGY.DOCX

MD (Doctor of Medicine) in Physiology

Tell me about MD (Doctor of Medicine) in Physiology

MD (Doctor of Medicine) in Physiology is a Non Clinical Speciality course. Doctor of Medicine in Physiology explores the studies of normal biological function, which provide the basis for understanding the abnormal function seen in human disease and for developing new methods for treating those diseases through translational research

. It is a three year postgraduation course and any MBBS degree holders from a University recognized by Medical Council of India can pursue this course. Physiologists can work in the departments of physiology as well as in some other departments of neurophysiology, pharmacology, cell biology, and biochemistry.

# MS MASTER OF SCIENCE IN ENTOTORHINLARYNGOLOGY.DOCX

MS (Master of Science) in ENT/Oto-Rhinlaryngology

Tell me about MS (Master of Science) in ENT/Oto-Rhinlaryngology

MS (Master of Science) ENT is a three-year post-graduate programme aimed at providing in-depth knowledge of diseases related to the ear, nose, throat and head and neck. The programme trains students to plan and advise measures for the promotive, precautionary, restorative and rehabilitative aspects of health and ailments in the speciality of ENT.

. Upon completion of the programme, the aspirants gain the ability to practice the speciality of surgery in keeping with the principles of professional ethics. In addition to mastering clinical expertise, the programme equips students' with the skills to manage the patients of trauma effectively.

Tell me about MS (Master of Science) in Obstetrics and Gynaecology

MS stands for Master of Science and MS in Obstetrics & Gynecology (OBGY) is offered by the Medical College & Research Centre, Teerthanker Mahaveer University.MS in Obstetrics & Gynaecology is a three-year postgraduation course

. Obstetrics and gynaecology (or obstetrics and gynecology; often abbreviated to OB/GYN, OBG, O&G is the medical specialty dealing with fields of obstetrics and gynaecology through only one postgraduate training program. This combined training prepares the practicing OB/GYN to be adept at the care of female reproductive organs health and management of obstetric complications, even through surgery

. The program provides adequate knowledge in clinical acumen, procedural skills and attitudes which will enable him/her to manage pregnancy and its complications, manage disorders affecting the female genital tract and problems in relation to human reproduction

. The candidates with a MBBS degree from a recognized institute, who have registered permanently with Medical Council of India or any other State Medical Councils, are eligible for this course.

# MS MASTER OF SCIENCE IN ORTHOPAEDICS.DOCX

MS (Master of Science) in Orthopaedics

Tell me about MS (Master of Science) in Orthopaedics

MS (Master of Science) Orthopaedics or Master of Surgery in Orthopaedics is a postgraduate Orthopaedics course. Orthopaedics is the branch of surgery concerned with acute, chronic, traumatic, and overuse injuries and other disorders of the musculoskeletal system

. Orthopaedic surgeons address most musculoskeletal ailments including arthritis, trauma and congenital deformities using both surgical and non-surgical means

. Orthopaedics covers that how to diagnose and treat diseases related to bones and joints such as all kinds of cervical spondylosis, bone tumour, spinal cord injury, rheumatoid arthritis, congenital diseases related to bones and joints, complex limb fractures and fractures that do not get healed. The course is career orienting in nature that provides many jobs after its completion in many fields.

Medical Laboratory Techniques (MLT) play a crucial role in healthcare diagnostics, research, and treatment. Suppose you are considering pursuing a Master's in this field

. In that case, Teerthanker Mahaveer University (TMU) in Moradabad offers an exceptional MSc in Medical Labs Techniques programme with academic excellence and a student-centric approach that makes this programme and the university stand out

. Also, In Medical Labs Techniques programme at TMU’s College of Paramedical Sciences stands among the top Paramedical colleges in India, ensuring that prospective students are well-informed about the programme and university offerings.

Frequently Asked Questions about MSc in Medical Laboratory Techniques

Q: Programme Details

Q: Programme Details

A: TMU's MSc In Medical Labs Techniques is a comprehensive programme designed to equip students with the knowledge and practical skills required in the dynamic healthcare landscape. The programme spans 2 years with a curriculum that covers a wide range of subjects, including advanced laboratory techniques, diagnostic procedures, and research methodologies.

Q: Full-Form of MSc In MLT

A: Understanding the full form of MSc is essential as MSc signifies a Master of Science in Medical Labs Techniques. This degree holds significance as it indicates a specialised and in-depth study of laboratory techniques in the medical field.

Q: Highlights of the Programme

A: What sets TMU's MSc programme apart are its unique highlights. The programme integrates advanced technology, practical training, and collaboration with healthcare institutions. Students benefit from equipped laboratories, experienced faculty, and industry-relevant projects, ensuring a holistic learning experience

.  Advanced Curriculum: The programme's curriculum is meticulously crafted to encompass the latest advancements in medical laboratory techniques. From theoretical foundations to hands-on training, students gain a comprehensive understanding of the field. Duration and Flexibility: TMU understands the importance of time for students

. The MSc programme is designed with an optimal duration, allowing for a balance between intensive learning and practical application. Experienced Faculty: The backbone of any educational programme is its faculty. TMU prides itself on having a team of experienced and dedicated professors who bring real-world insights into the classroom, enriching the learning experience

. Equipped Laboratories: Practical exposure is key in medical lab education. TMU provides access to advanced laboratories equipped with technology, enabling students to apply theoretical knowledge in a practical setting.

Q: Why Choose MSc In Medical Labs Techniques?

A: The healthcare industry is evolving, and the demand for skilled professionals in medical laboratories is on the rise. Pursuing MSc in Medical Labs Techniques opens doors to diverse career opportunities, including roles in diagnostic labs, research institutions, and healthcare organisations

. The programme not only enhances theoretical knowledge but also focuses on practical skills, making graduates industry-ready.

Q: Skills Required to Pursue MSc In Medical Labs Techniques

A: Teerthanker Mahaveer University’s MSc programme emphasises the development of skills such as laboratory techniques, data analysis, attention to detail, and effective communication. The curriculum is designed to nurture these skills, ensuring graduates are well-prepared for the challenges of the field with analytical skills, problem-solving, and decision-making.

Q: Why Choose M.Sc.(Nursing) in Obstetrics & Gynaecology Nursing?

. Nursing in Obstetrics and Gynaecology Nursing offers a chance for those who want to achieve expert status in the most important section of healthcare

. Obstetrics and gynaecology deal with aspects related to women's health in pregnancy, child delivery

, child delivery, and disorders in the reproductive system. This postgraduate programme offers immense knowledge in these critical areas and thus prepares the graduates with all the skills needed to bring positive change to the health and quality of life of women.Career Advancement OpportunitiesThe programme does lead to different types of advanced professional careers

. After graduation, the students are directed into a Clinical Nurse Specialist, Nurse Educator, or Supervisor position in obstetrics and gynaecology. This ensures that one's job is not only satisfying as a career but also brings responsibility and the power to make changes in care and practice in healthcare in general

. . Advanced subjects that will be introduced to the participants include high-risk obstetrics, neonatal care, and gynaecological disorders. This intensive training would surely prepare graduates for the management of complex cases and the provision of quality patient care

. You will be taken through practical training in affiliated hospitals and simulation laboratories for the acquisition of the following key skills necessary for real problem-solving in obstetrics and gynaecology

. Studying in this way bridges the gap between classroom learning and dealing with patients

, thus preparing you better for a challenge at any clinical level. Contribution to Women's Health Specialisation in obstetrics and gynaecology exposes one to an important position that improves health outcomes among women. The competencies and knowledge acquired therefore enable the provision of the highest standard of care during pregnancy, labor, and the postpartum period

. Such speciality knowledge empowers one to manage complications, support the patient through periods of critical illness, and promote overall well-being. It may not only be a very rewarding career path, one that comes with great personal and professional fulfillment but also a very much needed field focusing on women's health in health care.

Q: M.Sc.(Nursing) in Obstetrics & Gynaecology Nursing Programme Curriculum

A: The M.Sc. (N) in Obstetrics & Gynaecology Nursing at TMU is a two-year programme, divided into four semesters. Each semester is meticulously structured to provide both theoretical knowledge and practical experience. The curriculum is designed to cover essential subjects in the first year, laying a strong foundation in advanced nursing practices

. The second year focuses on specialisation in Obstetrics & Gynaecology, allowing students to delve deeper into the complexities of women’s health and maternal care.Year 1: Foundational CoursesIn the first year, students will engage with core subjects such as Advanced Nursing Practice, Research Methodology, and Nursing Education

. These courses provide a solid base in nursing theory and practice, preparing students for the advanced topics they will encounter in their specialisation.Year 2: Advanced Specialisation in Obstetrics & GynaecologyThe second year is dedicated to the specialisation in Obstetrics & Gynaecology Nursing

. Courses in this year include Obstetric Nursing, Neonatal Nursing, Gynaecological Nursing, and High-Risk Obstetrics. These subjects are designed to provide in-depth knowledge and skills required to care for women during pregnancy, childbirth, and postpartum

, childbirth, and postpartum, as well as managing gynaecological issues.Key Topics CoveredAdvanced maternal and child health nursingManagement of high-risk pregnanciesNeonatal care and nursingGynaecological disorders and managementEthical and legal issues in obstetrics and gynaecology

# MSC MEDICAL IN ANATOMY.DOCX

MSc Medical in Anatomy

Tell me about MSc Medical in Anatomy

MSc Medical in Anatomy is a two-year postgraduate programme, divided into 4 semesters. The MSc Medical in Anatomy programme focuses on the comprehensive study of human anatomy

. Q: M.Tech Additive Manufacturing programme curriculum

A: The M.Tech in Additive Manufacturing at Teerthanker Mahaveer University is structured to provide a balance of theoretical knowledge and practical experience

. The programme includes core subjects, elective courses, and a research project, ensuring that students gain a holistic understanding of Additive Manufacturing.Core Subjects in M.Tech Additive ManufacturingAdditive Manufacturing Technologies: This subject covers the various Additive Manufacturing technologies, including Stereolithography (SLA), Selective Laser Sintering (SLS)

, Selective Laser Sintering (SLS), and Fused Deposition Modeling (FDM)

. Students learn how to select the appropriate technology for different applications.Materials Science and Engineering: Understanding the materials used in Additive Manufacturing is critical for ensuring the quality and durability of printed parts

. This subject explores the properties of metals, polymers, and composites used in Additive Manufacturing.Computer-Aided Design (CAD): CAD is a fundamental tool in Additive Manufacturing, allowing engineers to design complex parts with precision

. This subject teaches students how to use CAD software to create digital models that can be printed using AM technologies.Advanced Manufacturing Processes: This subject delves into the advanced manufacturing processes that complement Additive Manufacturing, such as hybrid manufacturing and post-processing techniques

, ensuring that students have a well-rounded understanding of the manufacturing lifecycleElectives in M.Tech Additive ManufacturingMetal Additive Manufacturing: This specialisation focuses on the use of metals in AM, which is particularly important in industries like aerospace and automotive

. Students learn about the challenges and solutions in metal AM, including issues related to material properties and process optimisation.Polymer Additive Manufacturing: Polymer AM is widely used for producing lightweight and flexible parts

. This specialisation covers the various types of polymers used in AM, their properties, and their applications in different industries.Bioprinting: Bioprinting is an emerging field within AM that involves printing living tissues and organs

. This specialisation explores the technologies and materials used in bioprinting, as well as the ethical and regulatory considerations.Research Labs and FacilitiesTeerthanker Mahaveer University offers advanced research labs equipped with the latest Additive Manufacturing technologies, allowing students to conduct cutting-edge research.

# PHARM D PB POST BACCALAUREATE.DOCX

Pharm D PB (Post Baccalaureate)

Tell me about Pharm D PB (Post Baccalaureate)

Pharm D (Post Baccalaureate) is a three-year advanced programme designed for those who have completed B Pharm

. This programme allows graduates of the B.Pharm to advance their education and clinical expertise by focusing on clinical pharmacy, patient care, and pharmaceutical research.  The curriculum includes core subjects like Advanced Pharmacology and Clinical Research

, along with practical training through internships. Pharm D (Post Baccalaureate) programme Eligibility requires a B.Pharm degree from the candidates, and after completion of the degree, graduates can pursue careers in clinical pharmacy, research, academia, and various roles within the pharmaceutical industry..

# POST BASIC BSC IN NURSING.DOCX

Post Basic BSc in Nursing

Tell me about Post Basic BSc in Nursing

Post Basic BSc Nursing is a three-year undergraduate programme which is designed for registered nurses who wish to advance their skills and knowledge in nursing practice. The programme is structured into four semesters, covering an extensive syllabus that includes subjects such as Nursing Foundation, Community Health Nursing, Medical-Surgical Nursing, Mental Health Nursing, and more

. To be eligible for the Post Basic BSc Nursing programme, Applicants must have completed a General Nursing and Midwifery (GNM) programme with the minimum aggregate score as required. Post Basic BSc Nursing programme graduates can look forward to diverse career opportunities in healthcare settings, including roles in hospitals, community health services, and educational institutions.

The Corporate Resource Centre (CRC) at TMU plays a crucial role in preparing students for placements and professional success. With over 2500+ placement offers, the CRC has helped students land jobs with packages as high as ₹60 LPA (national), ₹32 LPA (international), ₹20 LPA (CCSIT), and ₹15 LPA (MBA)

# TMU_ADMISSION_PROCESS_GUIDE

TMU Admission Process — Complete Guide
========================================

Q1: TMU mein admission kaise hota hai? What is the admission process?
Q2: Online apply kaise karein? How to apply online at TMU?
Q3: Admission ke liye kya documents chahiye?
Q4: Kya entrance exam dena zaroori hai?
Q5: Merit-based admission kaise milta hai?
Q6: Admission form ki fee kitni hai?
Q7: Last date kab hai admission ki?

Answer:

TMU mein admission lene ke liye aap online ya offline dono tarike se apply kar sakte hain:

STEP 1: Visit tmu.ac.in/apply aur online application form bharein.
STEP 2: Required documents upload karein:
  - 10th Marksheet
  - 12th Marksheet (ya equivalent)
  - Aadhaar Card
  - Passport size photo
  - Category certificate (agar applicable ho)
  - Migration/Transfer certificate
STEP 3: Application fee pay karein (online payment available hai).
STEP 4: Document verification hogi.
STEP 5: Fee payment karein aur seat confirm karein.

ADMISSION ROUTES:
- B.Tech: JEE Main score ya TMU Entrance Test (TMUEE) ya 12th merit.
- MBBS/BDS: NEET score mandatory hai.
- MBA: CAT/MAT/CMAT score ya TMU entrance test.
- Law (BA LLB/LLB): CLAT score ya TMU entrance.
- B.Sc Nursing: NEET score required.
- Other UG Programs: 12th marks merit-based ya CUET score.
- PG Programs: Graduation marks merit-based.

IMPORTANT:
- Admissions are generally open from January to August (subject to seat availability).
- Some courses have rolling admissions — pehle aao pehle paao.
- Counselor se baat karein availability ke liye: 1800-270-7373 (Toll-Free)
- Online apply: https://www.tmu.ac.in/apply

For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/admissions
Contact: admissions@tmu.ac.in | +91-591-2484444


# TMU_AGRICULTURE_PROGRAMS

College of Agriculture at TMU — BSc Agriculture
==================================================

Q1: TMU mein Agriculture course hai kya?
Q2: BSc Agriculture ki details batao.
Q3: BSc Agriculture ki fees kitni hai?
Q4: Agriculture mein admission kaise hota hai?
Q5: MSc Agriculture hai kya TMU mein?
Q6: Agriculture ke baad career options kya hain?
Q7: Agriculture mein practical training kahan hoti hai?
Q8: Farm facility hai campus mein?
Q9: ICAR affiliated hai TMU Agriculture college?
Q10: Agriculture mein government job milti hai?

Answer:

TMU ka College of Agriculture ek modern, research-oriented agriculture education provide karta hai. Campus mein dedicated agricultural farm aur laboratories hain.

PROGRAMS OFFERED:

1. B.Sc Agriculture (Hons) — 4-year Program
   - Duration: 4 years (8 semesters)
   - Eligibility: 12th pass with PCB (Physics, Chemistry, Biology) OR PCM, minimum 50% marks
   - Admission: Merit-based on 12th marks / CUET
   - Includes: Field training, rural awareness programs, industrial visits

2. M.Sc Agriculture — 2-year PG Program
   - Duration: 2 years (4 semesters)
   - Eligibility: B.Sc Agriculture with minimum 55% marks
   - Specializations:
     a) Agronomy
     b) Soil Science
     c) Plant Pathology
     d) Horticulture
     e) Entomology

KEY SUBJECTS:
- Crop Production & Management
- Soil Science & Soil Fertility
- Plant Pathology & Pest Management
- Horticulture (Fruits, Vegetables, Flowers)
- Agricultural Economics & Marketing
- Animal Husbandry & Dairy Science
- Seed Technology
- Agri-Business Management
- Farm Machinery & Power
- Organic Farming

KEY FEATURES:
- On-Campus Farm: Dedicated agricultural land for practical training
- Modern Labs: Soil testing lab, plant tissue culture lab, seed technology lab
- Field Visits: Government farms, agricultural research stations, rural areas
- READY Program: Rural Entrepreneurship Awareness Development Yojana
- Industry Exposure: Agri-tech companies, food processing units visits
- Research Projects: Final year research dissertation with faculty guidance

CAREER OPPORTUNITIES AFTER BSC AGRICULTURE:
- Agriculture Officer (Government — UPSC/State services)
- Bank Agricultural Field Officer (IBPS/SBI)
- Agronomist / Crop Specialist
- Agriculture Scientist (after M.Sc/PhD)
- Agri-Business Manager
- Food Processing & Quality Control
- Seed/Fertilizer Company Representative
- Farm Manager
- Agriculture Journalist
- Self-Employment: Farm ownership, nursery, organic farming

GOVERNMENT JOBS:
- ICAR (Indian Council of Agricultural Research) — Scientist posts
- State Agriculture Department — Agriculture Development Officer
- Banks — Agriculture Field Officer (AFO)
- FCI (Food Corporation of India)
- Krishi Vigyan Kendra — Subject Matter Specialist

For fee details, contact admissions: 1800-270-7373
For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/college-of-agriculture


# TMU_BCA_PROGRAM

BCA at TMU — Bachelor of Computer Applications
=================================================

Q1: BCA course ki details batao TMU mein.
Q2: BCA ki fees kitni hai?

Q4: BCA ke baad kya scope hai? Job lagti hai?

Q8: TMU mein BCA placement kaisa hai?
Q9: BCA kitne saal ka course hai?
Q10: BCA ke liye 12th mein kaunsa subject chahiye?

Answer:

TMU ka BCA (Bachelor of Computer Applications) program CCSIT (College of Computing Sciences & IT) ke under aata hai. Yeh ek popular UG course hai jo IT field mein career banana chahne wale students ke liye ideal hai.

PROGRAMS OFFERED:

1. BCA (Hons) — 3+1 year Program
   - Duration: 3 years (6 semesters) — BCA Hons
   - Duration: 4 years (8 semesters) — BCA Hons with Research
   - Eligibility: 12th pass (any stream) with minimum 45% marks
   - Preferred: Mathematics/Computer Science in 12th (but not mandatory)
   - Admission: Merit-based on 12th marks / CUET score

KEY SUBJECTS:
- Programming: C, C++, Java, Python, Web Development
- Database: SQL, DBMS, Oracle
- Networking: Computer Networks, Cyber Security basics
- Software Engineering: Project Management, Software Testing
- Modern Tech: Cloud Computing, AI/ML basics, Data Analytics
- Mathematics: Discrete Math, Statistics, Operations Research

BCA HONS WITH RESEARCH:
- 4th year dedicated to research project
- Students work on industry-relevant projects
- Publication opportunity in academic journals
- Strong foundation for higher studies (M.Tech/PhD)

KEY FEATURES:
- Modern Computer Labs: Latest hardware and software
- Industry Partnerships: Tie-ups with IT companies for live projects
- Hackathons & Coding Competitions: Regular events to build skills
- Placement Training: Aptitude, communication, and technical training by CRC
- Internships: Industry internships in 5th/6th semester

CAREER OPPORTUNITIES AFTER BCA:
- Software Developer / Web Developer
- Mobile App Developer
- Database Administrator
- System Analyst
- IT Consultant
- Cyber Security Analyst
- Cloud Computing professional
- Higher Studies: MCA at TMU or any other university

PLACEMENTS:
- TMU BCA students placed in TCS, Wipro, Infosys, HCL, Cognizant
- Average Package: ₹3-5 LPA for BCA graduates
- 100% Placement Assistance through CRC

For fee details, contact admissions: 1800-270-7373
For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/ccsit

# TMU_CAMPUS_LIFE_FACILITIES

TMU Campus Life and Facilities
================================

Q1: TMU campus kaisa hai? Tell me about the campus.
Q2: Campus mein kya kya facilities hain?
Q3: Sports facilities kya hain TMU mein?
Q4: Library kaisi hai? Kitni books hain?
Q5: WiFi hai campus mein?
Q6: Hospital hai campus mein?
Q7: ATM aur shopping ki suvidha hai?
Q8: Transport facility hai kya?
Q9: TMU mein events aur fests hote hain?
Q10: Campus safe hai kya? Security kaisi hai?

Answer:

TMU ka campus 140-acre ka green campus hai jo Delhi Road (NH-24), Moradabad mein located hai.

CAMPUS FACILITIES:
1. Central Library: 1,00,000+ books, e-journals, digital resources, reading rooms, WiFi
2. Wi-Fi Campus: Pure campus mein free WiFi available hai
3. Sports Complex: Cricket ground, Football field, Basketball court, Badminton, Swimming Pool, Indoor Gym, Athletics Track
4. Auditorium: 2000+ seating capacity ka modern auditorium
5. Hospital: TMU Medical College Hospital — 500+ beds, fully equipped, community service
6. Cafeteria & Food Courts: Multiple eating options — North Indian, South Indian, Fast Food
7. Hostels: Separate boys aur girls hostels, well-furnished rooms with cooler/AC options
8. 24x7 Security: CCTV cameras, security guards, gated campus — girls hostel pe strict monitoring
9. ATM & Post Office: Campus ke andar hi banking aur postal services
10. Shopping Complex: Daily essentials, stationery, photocopying — sab campus mein milta hai
11. Transport: University buses available hain Moradabad city ke different routes pe
12. Medical Facility: 24x7 emergency medical assistance within campus
13. Labs & Workshops: State-of-the-art laboratories for all engineering, medical, and science programs

CULTURAL & EVENTS:
- Annual Cultural Fest: "Mahaveer Mahotsav" — 3-day mega cultural event
- Technical Fest: Hackathons, coding competitions, robotics
- Sports Meet: Inter-college aur inter-university championships
- Annual Convocation
- Guest Lectures: Industry leaders aur academic experts by invite
- NSS & NCC: Social service aur national cadet corps activities

RAGGING:
- TMU ek 100% Ragging-Free Campus hai
- Anti-Ragging Committee active rehti hai
- "Didi-Bhaiya" culture hai — senior students bahut supportive hain
- Strict action against any ragging complaints

LOCATION & CONNECTIVITY:
- Moradabad Railway Station se 10-15 km
- Delhi se NH-24 pe 3-3.5 ghante drive
- Nearest Airport: Delhi IGI Airport (approx 170 km)
- Regular buses from Delhi, Lucknow, Bareilly available

For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/campus-life

   - Duration: 4 years (8 semesters)

- Art Workshops: Guest artists and professionals conduct workshops
- Field Visits: Art gallery visits, heritage site tours, outdoor sketching sessions
- Annual Art Exhibition: Student work displayed for public and industry
- Modern Tools: Digital art tablets, design software (Adobe Suite)
- Interdisciplinary Learning: Collaboration with Media, Architecture, Design teams

--------------------

2. Merit Scholarship: Based on 12th marks (>90%)
3. Sports Quota: For national/state level players
4. EWS/SC/ST concessions (as per government norms)
5. Sibling Discount: Available for siblings studying at TMU


# TMU_HOSTEL_FAQ_RAG.DOCX

TMU Hostel & Accommodation – FAQ 

General Hostel Information

Q: How many hostels does TMU have?

A: TMU has five hostels on campus — two for boys and three for girls — with a total capacity to accommodate 4600 students.

Q: What kind of rooms are available in TMU hostels?

A: Rooms are available in 2-seater, 3-seater, and 4-seater options. Each type comes with either attached or common bathroom options.

Q: What furnishings are provided in each hostel room?

A: Each room includes a bed, wardrobe, study table, chair, and a desert cooler. Rooms with air conditioning are also available for additional charges.

Q: Is Wi-Fi provided in hostels?

Q: Is Wi-Fi provided in hostels?

A: Yes, high-speed Wi-Fi is available across all hostels.

Q: Are the hostels safe?

A: Yes, hostels are under 24x7 security and surveillance.

Food & Dining

Q: What kind of food is served in the hostel mess?

A: Only pure vegetarian food is served. Non-vegetarian food is strictly prohibited on campus.

Q: Is food served in a mess or delivered to rooms?

A: Food is served in spacious dining halls within the hostels. Students are not allowed to take food or utensils outside the mess unless permitted by wardens.

Q: Are students responsible for clearing their utensils?

A: Yes, students must clean up after themselves by placing used utensils in the appropriate bins and disposing waste in designated trash drums.

Hostel Fees (2025–26 Academic Year)

Hostel Fees (2025–26 Academic Year)

Q: What is the hostel fee for 2-seater rooms with attached bathroom and cooler?

A: For Non-Jain students: ₹130,000 per year (₹102,000 lodging + ₹28,000 mess). For Jain students: ₹114,700 per year (₹86,700 lodging + ₹28,000 mess).

Q: What is the hostel fee for 2-seater rooms with common bathroom and cooler?

A: For Non-Jain students: ₹90,000 per year (₹62,000 lodging + ₹28,000 mess). For Jain students: ₹71,400 per year (₹43,400 lodging + ₹28,000 mess).

Q: What is the hostel fee for 3-seater rooms with attached bathroom and cooler?

A: For Non-Jain students: ₹95,000 per year (₹67,000 lodging + ₹28,000 mess). For Jain students: ₹84,950 per year (₹56,950 lodging + ₹28,000 mess).

Q: What is the hostel fee for 3-seater rooms with common bathroom and cooler?

A: For Non-Jain students: ₹80,000 per year (₹52,000 lodging + ₹28,000 mess). For Jain students: ₹64,400 per year (₹36,400 lodging + ₹28,000 mess).

Q: What is the hostel fee for 4-seater rooms with attached bathroom and cooler?

A: For Non-Jain students: ₹75,000 per year (₹47,000 lodging + ₹28,000 mess). For Jain students: ₹67,950 per year (₹39,950 lodging + ₹28,000 mess).

Q: What is the hostel fee for 4-seater rooms with common bathroom and cooler?

A: For Non-Jain students: ₹60,000 per year (₹32,000 lodging + ₹28,000 mess). For Jain students: ₹50,400 per year (₹22,400 lodging + ₹28,000 mess).

Q: Are there any discounts for Jain students?

A: Yes. Jain students receive a 30% exemption in lodging fees for common bathroom rooms and 15% exemption for attached bathroom rooms.

Facilities and Lifestyle

Q: What additional facilities are available in the hostel?

A: Facilities include a visitor's lounge, common room with TV, indoor games, study areas, water purifiers, water coolers, 24/7 power backup, solar-heated water supply, laundry services, gym, and access to the on-campus super specialty hospital.

Q: Are wellness activities available for students in hostels?

A: Yes. Regular yoga and meditation sessions are organized in the mornings and evenings.

Hostel Administration & Wardens

Q: Who manages the hostels?

A: Each hostel is managed by resident and non-resident wardens. They act as local guardians and help students with outstation permissions, academic and personal support, and hostel coordination.

Hostel Rules & Conduct

Q: Can students cook inside the hostel rooms?

A: No, cooking in hostel rooms is strictly prohibited.

Q: What is the curfew policy for students?

A: Male students must return to campus by 6:00 PM and be inside the hostel by 10:30 PM. Female students must return to campus by 4:00 PM and be in the hostel by 7:00 PM. All students are expected to be in their rooms by 11:00 PM.

Q: What is the rule for going out of station?

Q: What is the rule for going out of station?

A: Students must submit a leave form to the warden, attach a parent's consent letter, collect a gate pass, and register their exit with security. They must carry their ID card while leaving.

Q: Can students change or share rooms on their own?

A: No, room changes or sharing are only allowed with written permission from the warden within the first few days of room allocation.

Q: Is there a rule about damaging property?

A: Yes. Students damaging hostel property will bear the repair cost and may face disciplinary action.

Q: Are guests allowed inside the hostels?

Q: Are guests allowed inside the hostels?

A: Only parents/guardians can visit after permission. Guest accommodation (limited) is available on payment. Only female guests are allowed in girls' hostels.

Q: Can students bring valuables or large cash?

A: Students are advised against keeping large amounts of cash or valuables. They are responsible for their personal belongings.

Q: Is there a fine for extra electricity usage?

A: Yes. 100 units per month are free. Beyond that, students are charged ₹6 per unit.

Q: What are banned items in hostels?

A: Smoking, pan masala, alcohol, drugs, gambling, non-veg food, weapons, explosives, and loud music are strictly banned.

Q: Can wardens enter rooms at any time?

Q: Can wardens enter rooms at any time?

A: Yes. The Chief Warden or Warden can open rooms in case of violations or security concerns.

# TMU_LAW_PROGRAMS

College of Law & Legal Studies at TMU
========================================

Q1: TMU mein Law course hai kya? Tell me about Law programs.
Q2: BA LLB ki fees kitni hai?
Q3: LLB 3-year program ki details batao.
Q4: LLM ki fees aur duration kya hai?
Q5: Law mein admission kaise hota hai? CLAT chahiye?
Q6: TMU Law College ki faculty kaisi hai?
Q7: Law ke baad placement milta hai?
Q8: Law mein internship opportunity hai?
Q9: Moot Court facility hai TMU mein?
Q10: TMU ka Law College BCI approved hai kya?

Answer:

TMU ka College of Law & Legal Studies BCI (Bar Council of India) approved hai aur quality legal education provide karta hai.

PROGRAMS OFFERED:
1. BA LLB (Hons) — 5-year Integrated Program
   - Eligibility: 12th pass (any stream) with minimum 45% marks
   - Duration: 5 years (10 semesters)
   - Admission: CLAT score / TMU entrance / Merit-based

2. LLB — 3-year Program
   - Eligibility: Graduation in any discipline with minimum 45% marks
   - Duration: 3 years (6 semesters)
   - Admission: CLAT score / TMU entrance / Merit-based

3. LLM — Master of Law
   - Eligibility: LLB degree with minimum 50% marks
   - Duration: 1 year (2 semesters) or 2 years
   - Specializations: Constitutional Law, Corporate Law, Criminal Law

APPROVAL: Bar Council of India (BCI) approved

KEY FEATURES:
- Moot Court Room: Courtroom-style moot court for practice advocacy
- Legal Aid Clinic: Community service through legal awareness programs
- Library: Law journals, case studies, bare acts, digital law databases
- Internship: Mandatory internships with courts, law firms, NGOs
- Guest Lectures: Practicing lawyers, judges, and legal experts
- Debates & Seminars: Regular legal debates, paper presentations

CAREER OPPORTUNITIES AFTER LAW:
- Advocate / Lawyer (Court Practice)
- Corporate Lawyer (Company Law)
- Legal Advisor / Consultant
- Judge (after Judicial Services Exam)
- Legal Officer in Government/Private organizations
- Public Prosecutor
- Legal Analyst
- Human Rights Lawyer

For fee details, contact admissions team: 1800-270-7373
For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/college-of-law


# TMU_MBA_PROGRAMS_DETAILS

MBA at TMU — Master of Business Administration
==================================================

Q1: TMU mein MBA ki fees kitni hai?
Q2: MBA mein kaunse specializations hain?
Q3: MBA mein admission kaise hota hai? CAT chahiye?
Q4: MBA ke baad placement kaisa hai?
Q5: MBA Dual Specialization kya hai?
Q6: MBA ki duration kitni hai?
Q7: MBA ke liye minimum graduation marks kitne chahiye?
Q8: TMU MBA AICTE approved hai?
Q9: MBA mein internship hoti hai?
Q10: MBA ke baad kitni salary milti hai?

Answer:

TMU ka MBA program AICTE approved hai aur dual specialization option ke saath industry-ready managers taioyaar karta hai.

PROGRAMS OFFERED:

1. MBA (Dual Specialization) — 2-year Program
   - Duration: 2 years (4 semesters)
   - Eligibility: Graduation (any discipline) with minimum 50% marks
   - Admission: CAT / MAT / CMAT / XAT score OR TMU Entrance Test
   - Specializations (choose any 2):
     a) Marketing Management
     b) Finance Management
     c) Human Resource Management (HRM)
     d) International Business
     e) Operations Management
     f) Information Technology (IT)
     g) Business Analytics

2. MBA in Logistics & Supply Chain Management — 2-year Program
   - Duration: 2 years
   - Focus: Supply chain, warehousing, transportation management
   - Industry visits to logistics companies

3. MBA Corporate with Global Exposure — 2-year Program
   - Duration: 2 years
   - Unique: International exposure module with foreign university visit
   - Focus: Global business practices aur cross-cultural management

KEY FEATURES:
- AICTE Approved: MBA programs are AICTE approved
- Dual Specialization: Students choose 2 areas for broader career scope
- Case Study Method: Harvard-style case study teaching approach
- Industry Projects: Live projects with companies
- Summer Internship: Mandatory 6-8 week summer internship after 2nd semester
- Guest Lectures: CEOs, MDs, industry leaders weekly sessions
- Entrepreneurship Cell: Support for student entrepreneurs
- Management Fest & Competitions: Regular B-school competitions

PLACEMENT HIGHLIGHTS:
- Top Recruiters: Deloitte, Ernst & Young, HDFC Bank, ICICI, Amazon, Flipkart
- Average Package: ₹5-8 LPA for MBA graduates
- 100% Placement Assistance
- CRC (Corporate Resource Centre) provides placement training:
  - Group Discussion practice
  - Personal Interview coaching
  - Resume building workshops
  - Aptitude & Reasoning training

CAREER OPPORTUNITIES AFTER MBA:
- Marketing Manager / Brand Manager
- Financial Analyst / Investment Banker
- HR Manager / Talent Acquisition Specialist
- Operations Manager
- Business Consultant
- Supply Chain Manager
- Digital Marketing Manager
- Business Analyst
- Entrepreneur

NOTE ON FEES:
- For exact, current fee structure, contact admissions: 1800-270-7373
- Fee payment can be made semester-wise
- Education loan assistance available

For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/college-of-management


# TMU_NURSING_PROGRAMS

BSc Nursing at TMU — College of Nursing
==========================================

Q1: TMU mein Nursing course hai kya? BSc Nursing details batao.
Q2: BSc Nursing ki fees kitni hai TMU mein?
Q3: BSc Nursing mein admission kaise hota hai? NEET chahiye?
Q4: Post Basic BSc Nursing kya hai?
