Q7: TMU Nursing College INC approved hai?
Q8: Clinical training kahan hoti hai?
Q9: Nursing mein scholarship milti hai?
Q10: Hostel compulsory hai nursing students ke liye?

Answer:

TMU ka College of Nursing INC (Indian Nursing Council) aur UP State Nursing Council approved hai. Clinical training TMU Medical College Hospital (500+ beds) mein hoti hai jo campus ke andar hi hai.

PROGRAMS OFFERED:

1. B.Sc Nursing — 4-year Program
   - Eligibility: 12th pass (PCB — Physics, Chemistry, Biology) with minimum 45% marks
   - Age: 17 years minimum at time of admission
   - Admission: NEET score required
   - Duration: 4 years (8 semesters) + 6 months internship
   - Clinical Training: TMU Hospital (500+ beds) — Hands-on patient care experience

2. Post Basic B.Sc Nursing — 2-year Program
   - Eligibility: GNM (General Nursing & Midwifery) diploma + Registered Nurse
   - Duration: 2 years (4 semesters)
   - Admission: Merit-based

3. M.Sc Nursing — 2-year PG Program
   - Eligibility: B.Sc Nursing with minimum 55% marks + 1 year clinical experience
   - Duration: 2 years
   - Specializations:
     a) Medical-Surgical Nursing
     b) Obstetrics & Gynaecology Nursing
     c) Paediatric Nursing
     d) Psychiatry/Mental Health Nursing
     e) Community Health Nursing

APPROVAL: Indian Nursing Council (INC) approved, UP State Nursing Council approved

KEY FEATURES:
- Clinical Training at TMU Hospital: 500+ bed hospital on campus — real patient exposure
- Simulation Lab: Advanced nursing simulation laboratory for practical training
- Community Health Programs: Field visits to rural health centres
- Library: Nursing journals, reference books, digital resources
- Hostel: Dedicated nursing hostel with warden facility (generally compulsory for BSc Nursing)
- International Standards: Curriculum aligned with global nursing practices

CAREER OPPORTUNITIES AFTER NURSING:
- Staff Nurse (Government/Private hospitals)
- ICU/OT/Emergency Nurse Specialist
- Community Health Nurse
- Nursing Superintendent
- Nursing Educator/Professor
- Public Health Officer
- Military Nursing Service (MNS)
- Opportunities abroad (UK, USA, Australia, Gulf countries — after additional registration)

For fee details, contact admissions: 1800-270-7373
For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/college-of-nursing


# TMU_SCHOLARSHIP_FAQS.DOCX

Teerthanker Mahaveer University - Scholarship FAQs

Q: What is the objective behind TMU's scholarship programs?

A: At TMU, scholarships aim to reward meritorious and deserving students to ensure that financial constraints do not hinder their pursuit of higher education.

Q: How many scholarships or concessions can a student avail in total?

A: A student can avail the Academic Scholarship plus a maximum of three additional scholarships/concessions.

Q: Is there a fee concession for paying the course fee annually?

A: Yes, candidates who pay the full annual fee at once receive an additional 5% concession on net tuition fees. This is not available for half-yearly payments.

Q: Does TMU offer scholarships for Jain Studies?

Q: Does TMU offer scholarships for Jain Studies?

A: Yes, TMU offers special scholarships for students enrolled in various programs if they pursue Jain Studies.

Q: What is the fee waiver provided under the Jain Studies scholarship?

A: Eligible students can get 50% tuition fee waiver for specific programs, 20% for others, and hostel lodging fee waivers (30% common, 15% attached bathroom).

Q: Are there scholarships based on marks in qualifying exams?

A: Yes. Students securing 60–69.9% get 10%, 70–79.9% get 15%, 80–89.9% get 25%, and 90% & above get 50%.

Q: Is the entry-level scholarship applicable to all programs?

A: No, it excludes D.El.Ed. (BTC), collaborative programs, Dental, Medical, Allied Programs, and Agriculture.

Q: What scholarships are available for B.Tech CSE (IBM collaboration)?

A: Students securing 70–79.99% in 10+2 get 10%, 80–89.99% get 20%, 90% & above get 25%.

Q: Are there scholarships based on CUET scores?

A: Yes. CUET scores offer: 60–69.99% – 10%, 70–79.99% – 15%, 80–89.99% – 25%, 90% & above – 50%.

Q: What scholarships are available based on JEE (Main) and UP-CET ranks for B.Tech?

A: JEE (Main) ranks up to 15,000: 90%, 15,001–25,000: 50%, 25,001–50,000: 20%; similar for UP-CET.

Q: What scholarships are available for MBA/MCA aspirants with CAT/MAT/CMAT scores?

A: 90–95 percentile: 20%, 96–97 percentile: 40%, 98 & above: 100%.

Q: Are there scholarships for TMU alumni or Madan Swarup Inter College pass-outs?

A: Yes. 60–69.9%: 15%, 70–79.9%: 20%, 80–89.9%: 30%, 90% & above: 50%.

Q: Do wards of TMU staff receive any scholarships?

A: Yes. Chancellor’s Scholarship provides 20% tuition fee waiver per year for the entire program.

Q: Is there a sibling scholarship available?

A: Yes. A 10% tuition fee discount is provided to the sibling with the lower tuition fee, applicable only in the first year.

Q: Are there scholarships for national or international level sportspersons?

A: Yes. Olympic/World Level Gold: 100%, Silver/Bronze: 80%, Inter-varsity Zonal Medalists: 60%, Recognized national level participation: 15%.

Q: Are there scholarships for district or state-level players?

A: Yes. Cluster/State participation: 10%, District or trial-based players: 5%.

Q: How are sports scholarships awarded?

A: A Selection Committee reviews applications and trials to finalize awards.

Q: Are existing Polytechnic students eligible for a B.Tech scholarship?

A: Yes. They receive a 20% tuition fee discount per year for the entire B.Tech duration. Applies only to non-Jain students.

Q: Are there scholarships for differently-abled students?

A: Yes. Awarded on a case-by-case basis for the full program, based on the level of disability and valid certificate.

Q: Can multiple scholarships be availed at once?

A: A candidate can avail a maximum of 3 additional scholarships/concessions in addition to the Academic Scholarship.

Q: Are scholarships available for programs with duration of one year or less?

A: No, such programs are not eligible for scholarships.

Q: How is the percentage calculated for scholarship eligibility?

A: Percentage is computed based on English + 3 main subjects. Subject combinations vary by program.


# TMU_SCHOLARSHIPS_COMPLETE_GUIDE

TMU Scholarships and Fee Concessions — Complete Guide
========================================================

Q1: TMU mein scholarship milti hai kya?
Q2: Jain students ke liye kya concession hai?
Q3: Merit scholarship ki criteria kya hai?
Q4: Sports quota scholarship hai?
Q5: SC/ST/OBC ke liye kya discount hai?
Q6: Sibling discount milta hai TMU mein?
Q7: EWS students ke liye fee concession hai?
Q8: Scholarship kaise apply karein?
Q9: 12th mein kitne marks pe scholarship milti hai?
Q10: Education loan facility hai kya?

Answer:

TMU mein kayi tarah ki scholarships aur fee concessions available hain jisse students ki education affordable ho jaaye.

SCHOLARSHIP SCHEMES:

1. JAIN MINORITY SCHOLARSHIP
   - Eligibility: Students belonging to Jain community
   - Benefit: 50% tuition fee waiver
   - Documents: Jain community certificate from recognized authority
   - Application: At the time of admission

2. MERIT SCHOLARSHIP
   - For 12th Marks:
     * 95% aur upar: Special merit scholarship (up to 100% tuition fee waiver)
     * 90% - 94.99%: Significant fee concession
     * 85% - 89.99%: Partial fee concession
   - For competitive exam toppers (JEE, NEET top ranks): Special packages
   - Renewed annually based on academic performance at TMU

3. SPORTS QUOTA SCHOLARSHIP
   - Eligibility: National/State level sports achievements
   - Level: Fee concession based on level of achievement
   - Required: Sports certificates, medal certificates from recognized bodies
   - Sports: Cricket, Football, Basketball, Athletics, Badminton, etc.

4. GOVERNMENT SCHOLARSHIPS (Facilitating)
   - SC/ST/OBC scholarships (Government of UP/Central Government)
   - EWS (Economically Weaker Section) concessions
   - PM Vidyalaxmi scheme
   - TMU helps students apply for government scholarship portals

5. SIBLING DISCOUNT
   - Eligibility: If a sibling is already studying at TMU
   - Benefit: Fee concession on second child's admission
   - Documents: Sibling's TMU ID card and enrollment proof

6. EDUCATION LOAN ASSISTANCE
   - TMU has tie-ups with multiple banks for education loans
   - Banks: SBI, PNB, Bank of Baroda, HDFC Credila, Axis Bank
   - Loan process guidance provided by admission office
   - Documents required: Income proof, admission letter, fee structure

HOW TO APPLY:
- Declare scholarship eligibility at the time of admission
- Submit supporting documents to scholarship cell
- Merit scholarships are auto-applied based on 12th marks
- Jain scholarship requires community certificate
- Sports scholarship requires certificates of achievement
- Contact scholarship cell: scholarship@tmu.ac.in

IMPORTANT NOTES:
- Scholarships apply to TUITION FEE only (hostel/mess charges separate)
- Merit scholarship renewal depends on maintaining minimum CGPA
- Scholarships cannot be combined (only one scheme applicable at a time)
- 50% Jain scholarship is the most availed scholarship at TMU

For more info, contact: 1800-270-7373 or visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in/scholarships


# TMU_UNIVERSITY_OVERVIEW

TMU University Overview — Why Choose TMU?
============================================

Q1: TMU kya hai? Tell me about TMU.
Q2: TMU kahan hai? Where is TMU located?
Q3: TMU ki ranking kya hai?
Q4: TMU government university hai ya private?
Q5: TMU ko kaunse approvals hain?
Q6: Why should I choose TMU?
Q7: TMU mein kitne colleges hain?
Q8: TMU mein total kitne students hain?
Q9: TMU ka campus kitna bada hai?
Q10: TMU ki fees affordable hai kya?

Answer:

Teerthanker Mahaveer University (TMU) ek leading private university hai jo Moradabad, Uttar Pradesh, India mein located hai.

KEY FACTS:
- Established: 2008 (Uttar Pradesh State Legislature Act)
- Campus: 140-acre green campus, Delhi Road (NH-24), Moradabad
- Accreditation: NAAC 'A' Grade
- Approvals: UGC, AICTE, BCI, PCI, NCTE, NMC (formerly MCI), DCI, INC approved
- Total Colleges: 14+ constituent colleges
- Programs: 200+ courses across UG, PG, Diploma, and Doctoral levels
- Students: 15,000+ students from across India and abroad

TMU KE 14 COLLEGES:
1. College of Computing Sciences & IT (CCSIT) — B.Tech CSE, BCA, MCA, M.Tech
2. College of Engineering (COE) — B.Tech Mechanical, Civil, Electrical, ECE
3. College of Management & Commerce — BBA, MBA, B.Com, M.Com
4. Teerthanker Mahaveer Medical College (TMMCRC) — MBBS, MD, MS
5. Teerthanker Mahaveer Dental College (TMDCRC) — BDS, MDS
6. College of Pharmacy — B.Pharm, M.Pharm, Pharm.D
7. College of Law & Legal Studies — BA LLB (5-year), LLB (3-year), LLM
8. College of Nursing — B.Sc Nursing, Post Basic B.Sc Nursing, M.Sc Nursing
9. College of Paramedical Sciences — BPT, BSc MLT, BSc RIT, Optometry
10. College of Education — B.Ed, B.El.Ed, B.P.Ed, M.P.Ed
11. College of Agriculture — B.Sc Agriculture, M.Sc Agriculture
12. College of Fine Arts — BFA (Bachelor of Fine Arts), MFA
13. College of Journalism — BJMC, MJMC
14. College of Applied Sciences — B.Sc, M.Sc (Physics, Chemistry, Math, Biotech)

WHY CHOOSE TMU?
1. NAAC 'A' Grade — Quality education ka guarantee
2. 140-acre green campus — Eco-friendly aur spacious environment
3. Highest Package: ₹60 LPA — Strong placement record
4. 700+ recruiters — TCS, Wipro, Infosys, Amazon, Adobe, Microsoft
5. International collaborations — Aivancity France, Global exposure programs
6. 500+ bed hospital — Medical facilities campus mein
7. Diverse programs — Engineering, Medical, Law, Management, Pharmacy, Agriculture
8. Jain values — Ethical aur value-based education
9. Affordable fees — Scholarship aur concessions available
10. Safe campus — 24x7 security, ragging-free, girl-friendly

INTERNATIONAL COLLABORATIONS:
- Aivancity (France) — M.Sc AI & Data Science joint programs
- Various MOUs with international universities for student exchange

For more info, visit: https://www.tmu.ac.in

Why Tmu
World Class
INFRASTRUCTURE

With a campus spanning over 130 acres, Teerthanker Mahaveer University is a dream destination where modern infrastructure, world-class facilities, and a supportive community create the perfect backdrop for your academic journey. Every corner of TMU is thoughtfully designed to inspire and support you, fostering a dynamic environment that complements both your academic and personal growth

. We offer a vibrant campus experience that blends learning with fun, featuring expansive auditoriums, well-furnished hostels, a gymnasium, and extensive sports arenas, including indoor and outdoor stadiums. TMU's 14 on-campus colleges offer a broad spectrum of academic programs, providing a comprehensive environment where students can thrive in all aspects of their lives.

Super speciality
Hospital
TMU Hospital is a leading centre for safety and advanced
healthcare,
offering a wide range of super-speciality services. It provides comprehensive primary, secondary,
and tertiary care, serving as a crucial healthcare resource for the community.
The hospital operates 24/7, with an 800+ bed super-speciality facility

on campus, ensuring round-the-clock medical care. It also offers hands-on practical training for
medical, nursing, and allied health students, allowing them to gain real-world experience in a
professional environment.
With comprehensive critical and emergency healthcare services, TMU Hospital
is equipped to handle a wide range of medical needs, making it a cornerstone of advanced medical

care in the region.
Centre for
Teaching, Learning & Development
Understanding that 88% of a candidate's success in corporate interviews is
based on soft skills, the Centre for Teaching, Learning and Development at TMU focusses on developing
essential life skills alongside academic knowledge. It offers training in quantitative, reasoning, and

verbal abilities, as well as enhancing interpersonal skills such as communication and teamwork. This
approach ensures students are well-rounded and ready for the demands of their future workplaces, making
them not only academically qualified, but truly prepared for real-world challenges and
opportunities.
Corporate Resource
Centre

opportunities.
Corporate Resource
Centre
The Corporate Resource Centre (CRC) at TMU is a specialised unit focused
on enhancing students' career prospects. It functions as a bridge between academic learning and
professional opportunities, offering services like career counselling, internship placements, and job

search assistance. It prepares students for the competitive job market by providing resources and
support for their career development, ensuring they are ready to excel in their chosen fields upon
graduation. Its success is reflected in its impressive 82% placement rate, showcasing its effectiveness
in guiding students toward fruitful career paths.

Centre

Business Incubation
Centre
TMU-BIC was established with a vision to foster entrepreneurship and
innovation, aligning closely with the Prime Minister's Startup India initiative. This vision aims to
create a supportive ecosystem to transform ideas into sustainable businesses, driving economic
growth and fostering self-reliance.
